module check-types

function check-types.all (data)

  • description and source-code
    function all(data) {
  if (array(data)) {
    return testArray(data, false);
  }

  assert.object(data);

  return testObject(data, false);
}
  • example usage
    ...
Supports nested objects.
Passing a single predicate
instead of an object
applies all of the values
to the same predicate,
ignoring nested objects.

* `check.all(results)`:
Returns `true`
if all the result values are true
in an array (returned from `apply`)
or object (returned from `map`).

* `check.any(predicateResults)`:
Returns `true`
...

function check-types.any (data)

  • description and source-code
    function any(data) {
  if (array(data)) {
    return testArray(data, true);
  }

  assert.object(data);

  return testObject(data, true);
}
  • example usage
    ...

* `check.all(results)`:
  Returns `true`
  if all the result values are true
  in an array (returned from `apply`)
  or object (returned from `map`).

* `check.any(predicateResults)`:
  Returns `true`
  if any result value is true
  in an array (returned from `apply`)
  or object (returned from `map`).

#### Some examples
...

function check-types.apply (data, predicates)

  • description and source-code
    function apply(data, predicates) {
  assert.array(data);

  if (isFunction(predicates)) {
    return data.map(function (value) {
      return predicates(value);
    });
  }

  assert.array(predicates);
  assert.hasLength(data, predicates.length);

  return data.map(function (value, index) {
    return predicates[index](value);
  });
}
  • example usage
    ...
that control
the message and type
of the thrown error object.
Also works with the `not`, `maybe` and `...of` modifiers.

#### Batch operations

* `check.apply(things, predicates)`:
Applies each value from the `things` array
to the corresponding predicate
and returns the array of results.
Passing a single predicate
instead of an array
applies all of the values
to the same predicate.
...

function check-types.array (data)

  • description and source-code
    function array(data) {
  return Array.isArray(data);
}
  • example usage
    ...
Duck-typing checker.
Returns `true`
if `thing` has all of the properties of `duck`,
`false` otherwise.

#### Array predicates

* `check.array(thing)`:
Returns `true`
if `thing` is an array,
`false` otherwise.

* `check.emptyArray(thing)`:
Returns `true`
if `thing` is an empty array,
...

function check-types.arrayLike (data)

  • description and source-code
    function arrayLike(data) {
  return assigned(data) && number(data.length);
}
  • example usage
    ...
`false` otherwise.

* `check.nonEmptyArray(thing)`:
Returns `true`
if `thing` is a non-empty array,
`false` otherwise.

* `check.arrayLike(thing)`:
Returns `true`
if `thing` has a numeric length property,
`false` otherwise.

* `check.iterable(thing)`:
Returns `true`
if `thing` implements the iterable protocol,
...

function check-types.assert (value, message, ErrorType)

  • description and source-code
    function assertImpl(value, message, ErrorType) {
  if (value === false) {
    throw new (ErrorType || Error)(message || 'Assertion failed');
  }
}
  • example usage
    ...
except it operates on iterables.

* `check.object.of.xxx(thing)`:
The `object.of` modifier
is synonymous with `array.of`,
except it operates on an object's properties.

* `check.assert(value, message, ErrorType)`:
Throws a `TypeError`
if `value` is `false`.
`message` and `ErrorType`
are optional arguments
that control
the message and type
of the thrown error object.
...

function check-types.assert.assigned ()

  • description and source-code

    function between(data, x, y) {

function check-types.includes (data, value)

  • description and source-code
    function includes(data, value) {
  var iterator, iteration;

  if (not.assigned(data)) {
    return false;
  }

  try {
    if (typeof Symbol !== 'undefined' && data[Symbol.iterator] && isFunction(data.values)) {
      iterator = data.values();

      do {
        iteration = iterator.next();

        if (iteration.value === value) {
          return true;
        }
      } while (! iteration.done);

      return false;
    }

    Object.keys(data).forEach(function (key) {
      if (data[key] === value) {
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return true;
  }

  return false;
}
  • example usage
    ...
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` implements the iterable protocol,
  `false` otherwise.
  In pre-ES6 environments,
  this predicate falls back
  to `arrayLike` behaviour.

* `check.includes(thing, value)`:
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` includes `value`,
  `false` otherwise.

function check-types.instance (data, prototype)

  • description and source-code
    function instance(data, prototype) {
  try {
    return instanceStrict(data, prototype) ||
      data.constructor.name === prototype.name ||
      Object.prototype.toString.call(data) === '[object ' + prototype.name + ']';
  } catch (error) {
    return false;
  }
}

function check-types.like (data, archetype)

  • description and source-code
    function like(data, archetype) {
  var name;

  for (name in archetype) {
    if (archetype.hasOwnProperty(name)) {
      if (data.hasOwnProperty(name) === false || typeof data[name] !== typeof archetype[name]) {
        return false;
      }

      if (object(data[name]) && like(data[name], archetype[name]) === false) {
        return false;
      }
    }
  }

  return true;
}
  • example usage
    ...
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` is an instance of `prototype`,
  `false` otherwise.
  Falls back to testing
  `constructor.name` and `Object.prototype.toString`
  if the `instanceof` test fails.

* `check.like(thing, duck)`:
  Duck-typing checker.
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` has all of the properties of `duck`,
  `false` otherwise.

function check-types.not (value)

    function notImpl(value) {
  return !value;
}
  • example usage
    ...
* `check.function(thing)`:
Returns `true`
if `thing` is a function,
`false` otherwise.

#### Modifiers

* `check.not(value)`:
Returns the negation
of `value`.

* `check.not.xxx(...)`:
Returns the negation
of the predicate.

module check-types.all

function check-types.all (data)

  • description and source-code
    function all(data) {
  if (array(data)) {
    return testArray(data, false);
  }

  assert.object(data);

  return testObject(data, false);
}
  • example usage
    ...
Supports nested objects.
Passing a single predicate
instead of an object
applies all of the values
to the same predicate,
ignoring nested objects.

* `check.all(results)`:
Returns `true`
if all the result values are true
in an array (returned from `apply`)
or object (returned from `map`).

* `check.any(predicateResults)`:
Returns `true`
...

module check-types.any

function check-types.any (data)

  • description and source-code
    function any(data) {
  if (array(data)) {
    return testArray(data, true);
  }

  assert.object(data);

  return testObject(data, true);
}
  • example usage
    ...

* `check.all(results)`:
  Returns `true`
  if all the result values are true
  in an array (returned from `apply`)
  or object (returned from `map`).

* `check.any(predicateResults)`:
  Returns `true`
  if any result value is true
  in an array (returned from `apply`)
  or object (returned from `map`).

...

function check-types.apply ()

  • description and source-code

  • example usage
    ...
that control
the message and type
of the thrown error object.
Also works with the `not`, `maybe` and `...of` modifiers.

#### Batch operations

* `check.apply(things, predicates)`:
Applies each value from the `things` array
to the corresponding predicate
and returns the array of results.
Passing a single predicate
instead of an array
applies all of the values
to the same predicate.
...

module check-types.array.of

function check-types.array.of.array ()

  • description and source-code
    array = function () {
  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

  try {
    collection.forEach(function (item) {
      if (
        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}
  • example usage
    ...

  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

  try {
    collection.forEach(function (item) {
      if (
        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}

`false` otherwise.

function check-types.arrayLike.of.boolean ()

  • description and source-code
    boolean = function () {
  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {

  }

  return true;
}

function check-types.arrayLike.of.match ()

  • description and source-code
    match = function () {
  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

  try {
    collection.forEach(function (item) {
      if (
        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}

module check-types.assert

function check-types.assert (value, message, ErrorType)

  • description and source-code
    function assertImpl(value, message, ErrorType) {
  if (value === false) {
    throw new (ErrorType || Error)(message || 'Assertion failed');
  }
}
  • example usage
    ...
except it operates on iterables.

* `check.object.of.xxx(thing)`:
The `object.of` modifier
is synonymous with `array.of`,
except it operates on an object's properties.

* `check.assert(value, message, ErrorType)`:
Throws a `TypeError`
if `value` is `false`.
`message` and `ErrorType`
are optional arguments
that control
the message and type
of the thrown error object.
...

function check-types.between (data, x, y)

  • description and source-code
    function between(data, x, y) {
  if (x < y) {
    return greater(data, x) && less(data, y);
  }

  return less(data, x) && greater(data, y);
}

module check-types.includes

function check-types.includes (data, value)

  • description and source-code
    function includes(data, value) {
  var iterator, iteration;

  if (not.assigned(data)) {
    return false;
  }

  try {
    if (typeof Symbol !== 'undefined' && data[Symbol.iterator] && isFunction(data.values)) {
      iterator = data.values();

      do {
        iteration = iterator.next();

        if (iteration.value === value) {
          return true;
        }
      } while (! iteration.done);

      return false;
    }

    Object.keys(data).forEach(function (key) {
      if (data[key] === value) {
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return true;
  }

  return false;
}
  • example usage
    ...
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` implements the iterable protocol,
  `false` otherwise.
  In pre-ES6 environments,
  this predicate falls back
  to `arrayLike` behaviour.

* `check.includes(thing, value)`:
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` includes `value`,
  `false` otherwise.

module check-types.instance

function check-types.instance (data, prototype)

  • description and source-code
    function instance(data, prototype) {
  try {
    return instanceStrict(data, prototype) ||
      data.constructor.name === prototype.name ||
      Object.prototype.toString.call(data) === '[object ' + prototype.name + ']';
  } catch (error) {
    return false;
  }
}

    function iterable(data) {
  if (typeof Symbol === 'undefined') {

module check-types.iterable.of

function check-types.iterable.of.array ()

  • description and source-code
    array = function () {
  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

  try {
    collection.forEach(function (item) {
      if (
        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}

        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}

function check-types.iterable.of.positive ()

  • description and source-code
    positive = function () {
  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

  try {
    collection.forEach(function (item) {
      if (
        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}

module check-types.like

function check-types.like (data, archetype)

  • description and source-code
    function like(data, archetype) {
  var name;

  for (name in archetype) {
    if (archetype.hasOwnProperty(name)) {
      if (data.hasOwnProperty(name) === false || typeof data[name] !== typeof archetype[name]) {
        return false;
      }

      if (object(data[name]) && like(data[name], archetype[name]) === false) {
        return false;
      }
    }
  }

  return true;
}
  • example usage
    ...
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` is an instance of `prototype`,
  `false` otherwise.
  Falls back to testing
  `constructor.name` and `Object.prototype.toString`
  if the `instanceof` test fails.

* `check.like(thing, duck)`:
  Duck-typing checker.
  Returns `true`
  if `thing` has all of the properties of `duck`,
  `false` otherwise.

    function map(data, predicates) {
  assert.object(data);

  if (isFunction(predicates)) {
    return mapSimple(data, predicates);
  }

  assert.object(predicates);

module check-types.number

function check-types.number (data)

  • description and source-code
    function number(data) {
  return typeof data === 'number' &&
    isNaN(data) === false &&
    data !== Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY &&
    data !== Number.NEGATIVE_INFINITY;
}

module check-types.object.of

function check-types.object.of.array ()

  • description and source-code
    array = function () {
  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

  try {
    collection.forEach(function (item) {
      if (
        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}
  • example usage
    ...
Duck-typing checker.
Returns `true`
if `thing` has all of the properties of `duck`,
`false` otherwise.

function check-types.object.of.instanceStrict ()

  • description and source-code
    instanceStrict = function () {
  var collection, args;

  collection = arguments[0];

  if (target === 'maybe' && not.assigned(collection)) {
    return true;
  }

  if (!type(collection)) {
    return false;
  }

  collection = coerceCollection(type, collection);
  args = slice.call(arguments, 1);

  try {
    collection.forEach(function (item) {
      if (
        (target !== 'maybe' || assigned(item)) &&
        !predicate.apply(null, [ item ].concat(args))
      ) {
        // TODO: Replace with for...of when ES6 is required.
        throw 0;
      }
    });
  } catch (ignore) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}
